Anti-Smoking and Anti-Drug Propaganda Week: Cai Jingjun's Broadcast Speech, Xia Zhongming Represents the Broadcast 154

A Central News Agency report: Yesterday was the broadcast propaganda day for Anti-Smoking and Anti-Drug Propaganda Week. From 4:00 PM to 4:30 PM, Cai Jingjun, Director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, specially sent Xia Zhongming, Director of the Audit Section of the Fourth Division, to represent him at the Zhongxi Radio Station to broadcast a very detailed explanation of the significance of anti-smoking. The original script of the broadcast is recorded below.

Fellow citizens of this city, from the 20th to the 26th of this month is the expanded Anti-Smoking and Anti-Drug Propaganda Week. Why is this expanded Anti-Smoking and Anti-Drug Propaganda Week designated? It is to expand the propaganda about the scourge of opium and drugs, so that all residents of the city understand the threat of opium and drugs to the survival of the nation and the people, arouse the attention of citizens, and awaken opium addicts, work together to eliminate opium and drugs, and consolidate the survival of the nation and the people.

Its significance is very important. China has suffered from the scourge of opium and drugs for hundreds of years, and in the past hundred years, the harm has been even deeper, almost jeopardizing the survival of the entire country and nation. All people with knowledge and insight are heartbroken. Speaking of the history of opium prohibition in China, it can be said to be three hundred years old. Since the Qianlong period of the Qing Dynasty and up to the establishment of the Republic of China, and the period when the Northern Warlords were in power, opium prohibition orders have been promulgated. Among them, the methods adopted by Lin Zexu in Guangdong during the Daoguang period were the most severe, which led to the Opium War and the signing of unequal treaties, which had the greatest impact on our national status. Therefore, examining the results of our country's past opium prohibition efforts, they have all failed. What is the reason for the failure? Because the people who advocated opium prohibition in the past only knew that opium should be prohibited, but did not know how to seek methods to prohibit it. Because the methods of prohibition were not proper, there was no effect, and the result was failure. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, in view of the disaster of opium, which is more severe than before, and that if it is not prohibited as soon as possible, the country and the nation will be plunged into a position of no return, so he stipulated a

Six-Year Opium Prohibition plan, and detailed the prohibition plan, adopting appropriate methods to make it easy to implement and achieve the effect of completion within a limited time. The current method of opium prohibition considers all four aspects of planting, transportation, smoking, and selling. Because if only smoking is prohibited but planting, transportation, and selling are not prohibited, then the planters will plant, the transporters will transport, and the sellers will sell, and the effectiveness of smoking prohibition will be offset. The reverse is also true. Therefore, planting, transportation, selling, and smoking should all be carried out simultaneously, with smoking prohibition as the center. The first step in opium prohibition is to register opium addicts, so that all people who smoke opium are registered. Then, we can know how many opium addicts there are in each province and city, and how much they smoke. We can get statistics, know the total number of opium addicts, and use it as a standard for phased rehabilitation. Knowing the total amount of smoking can be used as a method for controlling planting, transportation, and selling. Therefore, with a standard for phased rehabilitation of opium addicts, there is also a method for phased reduction of planting, transportation, and selling. When opium addicts are completely rehabilitated, then planting, transportation, and selling can be completely prohibited. Therefore, opium prohibition must involve planting, transportation, selling, and smoking

simultaneously in order to achieve results. As mentioned above, smoking is the center of opium prohibition, and the first step in smoking prohibition is the registration of opium addicts. The registration method is now being actively promoted throughout the country. This city started registration in July last year and ended at the end of December. The number of registered opium addicts is 30,833. However, according to the investigation and the estimates of special industry associations, the number of unregistered opium addicts is large. Because unregistered opium addicts are worried about being detained and sentenced when they cannot obtain a license after the registration deadline, although this is due to the fact that opium addicts do not understand the significance of registration, it also affects the future of opium prohibition, because if opium addicts do not fully register according to law, the total number of opium addicts and the total amount of smoking cannot be accurately counted, then the control of planting, transportation, and selling cannot be carried out. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, who is also the Opium Prohibition Commissioner, because the registration of opium addicts in various provinces and cities has not been widespread, has recently ordered the provinces and cities to implement a general inspection of opium addicts, and has specially appointed commissioners to handle it jointly with the provinces and cities, and has also promulgated a kind of reporting opium addicts,

Registration Methods. The content of the registration methods for reporting opium addicts includes sending police officers to inspect households to check for opium addicts. If there are unregistered opium addicts, they will be ordered to register. At the same time, unregistered opium addicts are allowed to register retroactively and will not be prosecuted for the time being. This method can be said to be a compassionate measure taken by the government to show consideration for opium addicts and give them a chance to start anew, thinking about the interests of opium addicts. Being able to get this opportunity to register retroactively and avoid the law is a very rare opportunity. If you miss this opportunity to register retroactively, it will be more difficult to find another opportunity to register than to reach the sky. Therefore, it is hoped that unregistered opium addicts will quickly apply to the Public Security Bureau and branch offices to register during the period when reporting opium addicts is allowed to register retroactively. If you continue to delay and fail to register according to the regulations, after the three-month deadline expires, smoking opium without a license will be treated as illegal private smoking. If illegal private smokers are found by the inspectors of this bureau, they will be arrested and sent to the headquarters for trial according to the Provisional Regulations for the Punishment of Opium Prohibition Offenses, without leniency. Opium addicts, pay attention, this is the

Last Time for registration, hurry up to register retroactively, don't make a mistake and regret it later. The registered opium addicts and the amount of smoking should be rehabilitated in phases and reduced in phases according to regulations, with six months as one phase, that is, a portion of the registered opium addicts should be rehabilitated in the first six months, and those who cannot be rehabilitated in the first six months should also appropriately reduce the amount of smoking, so those who cannot be rehabilitated should exchange for an opium cessation license and temporarily smoke, and then gradually reduce the amount of opium until rehabilitation. Therefore, in the strict implementation of the opium cessation regulations, there is a provision for a limited-term opium cessation license, which must be exchanged every month. This city started registration in July 24 and ended at the end of December. The six-month validity period of all opium cessation licenses issued has expired. According to regulations, new licenses must be exchanged. Therefore, from April 1st to May 31st, it is the period for opium addicts in this city to exchange for the second phase of licenses. If it passes

May 31st and you have not come to register to exchange for a new license, then the old license you previously obtained will be invalidated. Smoking opium in the future will be considered illegal private smoking. Opium addicts who smoke illegally and privately will be arrested if found by the investigators of this bureau and sent to the headquarters for trial according to law. The penalty and punishment will be in accordance with Article 8 of the Provisional Regulations for the Punishment of Opium Prohibition Offenses, which stipulates imprisonment for not less than six months and not more than two years, and may be subject to a fine of not more than 300 yuan. It is hoped that opium addicts who have obtained the first phase of licenses will comply with the prescribed time limit and quickly go to the bureau to apply for license exchange registration. As for the procedures for license exchange, they have already been announced in the newspapers.

The main purpose of handling opium addict registration and issuing limited-term opium cessation licenses is to obtain the total number of opium addicts as a standard for phased rehabilitation. The purpose is still

Phased Opium Cessation to achieve the purpose of prohibition. However, opium addicts who are old and deeply addicted and cannot be rehabilitated immediately will be issued licenses to smoke temporarily, so that their amount of smoking will gradually decrease until they are rehabilitated. Therefore, the method of rehabilitation is relatively gentle and the time is longer. This is a kind of painstaking effort of the government to show understanding for those who are old and whose addiction cannot be rehabilitated immediately. It does not mean that once you obtain a license, you can smoke opium permanently without having to rehabilitate. If opium addicts have this kind of idea, then they have completely misunderstood the government's painstaking efforts and intentions. Therefore, if opium addicts can understand the government's determination to prohibit opium and voluntarily go to the Public Security Bureau to request to be sent to rehabilitation, not only will we praise them, but we will also welcome them extremely. This city has three municipal opium cessation hospitals and one temporary drug rehabilitation center. The facilities are very complete and the technology is very proficient, and

All Expenses are borne by the municipal government, and opium addicts do not need to pay fees. Therefore, opium addicts who are willing to rehabilitate immediately can voluntarily request to be sent to rehabilitation. This is the best opportunity for opium addicts to quit opium. If opium addicts voluntarily pay for opium cessation, the Health Bureau and the Public Security Bureau will designate 17 hospitals with complete equipment and excellent technology, where they can also be admitted to the hospital for opium cessation. After obtaining a certificate of rehabilitation, they can submit it to the Public Security Bureau for record, and it can be considered that they have successfully quit opium addiction. Therefore, opium addicts who can recognize the government's opium prohibition policy and determination and can quit opium immediately are truly praised by the government.

After I have explained the government's opium prohibition policy and opium prohibition methods, I hope that opium addicts who smoke opium will have a thorough understanding, and citizens will have a thorough understanding,

Understanding Recognition. We must make the Chinese nation survive permanently in the world, and the Republic of China stand permanently among nations. We must make a fierce attack on the opium and drugs that endanger our permanent survival and completely eliminate them. We also hope that opium addicts will abide by the laws and regulations set by the government and strive to rehabilitate themselves as soon as possible, have a complete personality, and still be a good citizen of the country. This is my fervent hope. Citizens, let us unite and work hard to promote the anti-smoking and anti-drug movement. Citizens, abide by the government's laws and regulations, eliminate lifelong pain, and regain future happiness.

Tragic Explosion at Zhabei York Refrigeration Plant; Worker Zhu Tingdou Blown to Pieces and Killed; Five Injured Receiving Treatment, Lives Not in Danger 155

The British-owned York Refrigeration Plant at No. 29 Quanji'an Road, Xiangyan Bridge, Zhabei, has a factory next to it at No. 13 Lane. When machine parts are damaged, they are repaired by hired craftsmen using electric ironing methods at any time. Yesterday at 3:30 PM, a craftsman from the factory, Zhu Tingbao, 26 years old, from Wuxi, residing at No. 255 Qipu Road, was using a current device to repair a refrigeration iron machine part. Suddenly, the refrigeration cylinder burst with a loud explosion like thunder. Iron fragments flew everywhere. Zhu was working with his head lowered and was knocked to the ground by the explosion. Both arms and legs were severed from his torso, and blood and flesh splattered, a truly tragic sight. He died on the spot. Those who were injured in the head, face, hands, feet, chest, abdomen, etc., included Yan Qianlang, Yang Xiaodi, Wang Asan, Lin Quansheng, and Zhao Mugen, a total of five people. They were bleeding profusely and moaning in pain. The police officer on duty found out and reported to the Linping Road Police Station. An ambulance was called to send the five injured people to Tongren Hospital for treatment. Their injuries were not serious. The police station sent police officers to investigate the scene and ordered the local bailiff to report to the local court, which dispatched a prosecutor to the scene today to examine the body of Zhu Tingbao, who was killed in the explosion. At the same time, the factory will provide generous compensation to the family of the deceased.

Explosion in Wusong Foundry Causes Disaster; Five Men and Women Injured; Minor Injuries, Already Discharged 156

Yu Shunxing Foundry at No. 19 Changnan Road, East City, Wusong, specializes in casting copper sheaves for sailboat rigging. Yesterday, the owner of the shop went to Shanghai to sell goods. Only two apprentices were left in the shop. At around 3 PM, an old goods vendor brought a copper box shaped like a cigarette can for sale. Lu Xiucheng, a 15-year-old apprentice from Taizhou, gave him four small dollars and accepted it, but he did not know that the box was a bomb. Lu was dismantling the box at the door when the bomb suddenly exploded with a loud bang and sparks flying everywhere. The apprentice was the first to be hit, and a hole the size of a silver dollar was blown into his abdomen. An old woman named Pan Liu, 59 years old, who was setting up a fruit stall next door, was injured in the hand. Li Zhanglin, a clerk at Yuanshun Pig Bank, which was three or four doors away to the south, was injured in the leg. Xu Xinshun, a tax reporting agent, and Xu Baotang were injured in the leg. The farmer Yang Fulang was injured in the leg. After the incident, the five injured men and women were sent to the sanitation hospital. After the doctor bandaged them, they were discharged from the hospital because their injuries were minor. It is said that the explosive power of the bomb was not very strong, otherwise it might have caused a major disaster.

According to a Shanghai dispatch from the Wai Lun News Agency, a reporter from the Continental Daily obtained information yesterday afternoon from reliable sources that, since the arrest of three suspects in the case of the shooting death of Japanese sailor Nakayama Hideo, and after secret interrogation by the First Special Court, more suspects would be arrested. Yesterday, this newspaper published a news item stating that two suspects, said to be directly related to the Nakayama shooting, had been arrested by the police and sent to the Special District Court for secret trial. One of them was reportedly arrested in Tianjin and sent to Shanghai. The news in yesterday's newspaper also indicated that the police officers handling the case were keeping all details strictly confidential. It is now heard that a third person was arrested in Qingdao a few days ago and sent to Shanghai on Sunday. He was interrogated in court yesterday morning. Therefore, the secrecy of this case seems to have increased another layer. This third person and the two suspects arrested a few days ago were tried in the First Special Court at around 11 o'clock yesterday, presided over by Judge Feng Shide. No one was allowed to attend the hearing. Apart from the presiding judge, clerk, police officer, bailiff's lawyer, and the suspects, there were no other people. Zhang Tingrong, secretary of the municipal government, was present as an observer but refused to release any information about the case. The police authorities are keeping the case extremely secret. To avoid leaks, only a few police officers directly involved in the case know the progress of the case, but they are also keeping it strictly confidential. As for other police officers, most of them have no knowledge of the contents of the case. After the above three suspects were interrogated yesterday, they were escorted back to the Central Jail under strict guard in a car. When the suspects left the court, the crowds of onlookers were dispersed, and efforts were made to prevent reporters from seeing the faces of the suspects. Because it is only known that the above-mentioned arrested people are related to the Nakayama shooting case, and no other direct information has been leaked to the outside world, it has aroused a kind of speculation that the three arrested people are not Chinese. The reporter of the Continental Daily had a glimpse of the arrested suspects when they stepped out of the court after the trial on Monday and yesterday. In this glimpse, the reporter had an idea that there might be jurisdictional issues mixed in this case, so the trial was so secret. But this is just speculation and cannot be taken as fact. The Public Concession Engineering Bureau established a special investigation department in November last year after the case occurred to investigate the case, but the staff of the department refused to discuss the case with reporters yesterday.

Therefore, the two Chinese women are still in the VIP room of the headquarters. Director Cai also returned to Shanghai from Nanjing yesterday morning, and has also asked the municipal government for instructions regarding the request made by the Japanese Consulate.

According to the Greater Shanghai Evening Post, there are now six suspects detained and awaiting trial in the case of the Japanese sailor Nakayama who was killed on Binle Road in November last year. Three of them are Chinese, currently believed to be Cantonese, and are detained by the General Patrol Room of the Public Concession. Two other Chinese are detained by the Nanshi Public Security Bureau. There is also a Korean detained by the Police Department of the Japanese Consulate. The patrol room still does not want to release any information about the case, and the Chinese and Japanese authorities are also keeping their mouths shut. The reason is that the Chinese, Japanese, and Public Concession Police authorities are still cooperating to apprehend other suspects, and the true culprit in the case is also on the list of those being apprehended. According to reliable sources this morning, one of the three Cantonese was arrested in Tianjin last week and sent to Shanghai, one was arrested in Qingdao at the same time and also sent to Shanghai, and the third was arrested by the Dixiwei Road Patrol Room a few days ago. The first two were questioned by the First Special District Court on Sunday, and it was decided that the three would be interrogated together again. It is said that the hearing will continue on May 1. The Korean detained by the Japanese Consulate, nicknamed Jia Ke, is said to have come to China from Vladivostok and was arrested in Qingdao by the Public Concession detectives on April 15 along with the first two Cantonese. He was sent to Shanghai on Sunday and handed over to the Japanese Consulate for detention. It is said that all of them are accomplices, while the true culprit has not yet been arrested and is believed to be hiding in Qingdao. Yesterday, two women related to the case were arrested at the Yuegong Dance Hall on North Sichuan Road. One is a dancer named Chen, from Ningbo, 28 years old, who recently came to Shanghai from Qingdao. The other is a married Cantonese woman named Ye, 45 years old, who is involved in the operation of the Yuegong Dance Hall and Hotel. At around 5 PM yesterday afternoon, two Japanese officers went to the Nanshi Public Security Bureau to visit the director. Because the director had gone to Nanjing on official business, they were received by the secretary. The Japanese officers requested assistance in arresting the above-mentioned two women, but did not specify their names or addresses. So, the police chief and the detective chief led a team with the Japanese officers to the North Railway Station Branch and asked the director to go with them to arrest the suspects. They first went to a middle school in Zhabei but did not see anyone. Then, they traced their steps to the Yuegong Dance Hall and finally arrested the two women. The Japanese officers wanted to take the two women to the Japanese Consulate, but the Public Security Bureau officials refused. Later, at around 10 PM, the two women were taken to the Nanshi Public Security Bureau, and the Japanese officers still followed. They insisted on taking the two women to the Japanese Consulate, and finally left the bureau around midnight. The crimes committed by the two women are unknown, but it is known that their nature is very serious. It is believed that the two women hid the criminals in the case, hence their implication.

Bizarre Dice Gambling Dispute; Same Numbers on Both Sides, All Throws Are the Same; Friends Quarrel Over Gambling, Request Court Investigation 162

Zhu Yun'an, owner of the Shaoxing Xiang Board Box Shop at No. 46 Jiya Lane, Shandong Road, Wang Jinkun, owner of the Wang Shunxing Board Box Shop at No. 53 Jinlong Street, and Chen Baosheng (also known as Bao Sheng), owner of the Xianyilou Lamb Shop at No. 504 Fujian Road, were very good friends. In the first month of the lunar calendar this year, Chen opened a room at the Shanxi Road Nanjing Hotel for gambling Pai Gow. By March 18 of the solar calendar, Zhu owed 745 yuan, of which 700 yuan was in cash and 45 yuan in checks. Wang Jinkun owed 1,900 yuan in cash and 350 yuan in checks. At around 7 PM on the 18th of last month, they gathered again at the 703 room of the Nanjing Hotel to gamble Pai Gow, with Chen Baosheng as the dealer. A total of six Pai were pushed, and the dice thrown were all numbers such as three, seven, and eleven, without numbers such as two, four, six, eight, ten, twelve, five, and nine. Zhu and Wang became suspicious and took the dice off to investigate. Chen then forcibly snatched them, resulting in a dispute. In the end, Zhu and others took the dice and, upon inspection, found that the dice were different from ordinary ones. The numbers on both sides were the same, and any throw would result in numbers such as three, seven, and eleven. They were about to negotiate when Chen suddenly reported to the Patrol Room that Tang and Fang were extorting 30 yuan from him and wanted to detain these two people. To investigate, they had to question Zhu Yun'an and Wang Jinkun. The detectives then arrested Zhu and Wang and sent them to the First Special Court. After questioning, the Patrol Room did not prosecute Zhu and Wang and released them. At that time, the Patrol Room suspected Chen of fraud and reported to the court to take them back for investigation, but the result was also not to prosecute. Zhu and Wang, feeling very unhappy about being deceived, hired lawyer Tao Wuzhi to file a criminal lawsuit against Chen Baosheng for fraud in the First Special Court, requesting that he be punished for the crime under Article 339 of the Criminal Law, and filed a civil lawsuit demanding the return of the money owed. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Yang Qianchang opened the Second Criminal Court for questioning. The defendant hired lawyer Wang Shizong to defend him. According to his statement, there were only mahjong games at the time, not Pai Gow. Because the plaintiff had cheated, he argued with them, which led to today's incident. Judge Yang said that further investigation was needed and rescheduled the hearing.

Zhang Xiaogen Secretly Possessed a Handgun and Bullets; The Bullets Were Identical to Those Used in the Assassination Case; The First Special Court Sentenced Him to Two Years for Possessing Gun and Bullets; The Assassination Case Was Approved for Transfer to the Shanghai Public Security Bureau for Investigation 163

Ruan Yao, a Chinese detective of the Xinzha Police Station, arrested Zhang Xiaogen, a native of Changzhou, on the 16th of this month on Avenue Edward VII in Xinle Lane for secretly possessing firearms. A handgun and twenty bullets were confiscated and sent to the First Special Court, where he was prosecuted for the crime of possessing firearms. After an initial interrogation, he was ordered to be detained pending further investigation. It has now been learned that during the adjournment, the police station sent the confiscated gun and bullets to the Shanghai Municipal Council's Firearms Inspection Office for examination. It was discovered that the bullets were identical to those found on the body of Lu Rukang, who was shot and killed in an assassination on January 14th at No. 5 Renxing Lane, Qingyun Road, Zhabei. It was therefore determined that Lu Rukang was killed by the gun. Now that Zhang Xiaogen possessed the gun, he was suspected of involvement in the Lu Rukang murder case. The police station notified the Shanghai Public Security Bureau to send officers to take custody. Yesterday morning, the police station escorted Zhang Xiaogen to the Eighth Criminal Court of the First Special Court for further interrogation. Zhang Tianyin, the police station's lawyer, stated the above situation, and Gu Liancheng, the squad leader of the Shanghai Public Security Bureau's Detective Team, arrived at the court, submitting an official document stating that Zhang Xiaogen was found to be related to the Lu Rukang assassination case, requesting permission to transfer him for interrogation. When questioned, Zhang Xiaogen claimed that he had found the handgun in Nanxiang during the January 28th Incident. He denied committing the assassination. Judge Tan Xinzhen ruled that Zhang Xiaogen was sentenced to two years of imprisonment for possessing military firearms and ammunition without permission. He was first handed over to the Shanghai Public Security Bureau to be taken back for investigation. The gun and bullets were sent back to the police station for execution after the interrogation was completed.

Residents of Xujiahui Request the Municipal Government to Fill in the Zhaojiabang River; The River Water Turns Black – The Stench Reaches the Sky 164

Zhou Chengxiang and others, representatives of the Notre Dame Convent of the Catholic Church in Xujiahui, Shanghai, and all merchants and residents of Xujiahui Town, submitted separate petitions to the Municipal Government's Health and Social Affairs Bureaus yesterday, stating that the stench in the Pu Zhaobang River in the town was affecting public health. They requested that officials be sent to inspect the area as soon as possible and find ways to fill in the river to prevent epidemics. The petition stated, "We, the residents of the Notre Dame Convent of the Catholic Church in Xujiahui Town and along Xujiahui Road, live on both sides of the Zhaojia Hong River. Since the Pu Zhaobang River was dredged the year before last, the foul water from the east has flowed in. We have built a dam west of the Tian Bridge to block the foul water and divert clear water from the south, which has greatly benefited the residents of the western countryside. However, outside the wall of the Notre Dame Convent, there is a place where the foul water is blocked. Since the river is cut off here, the foul water from the east cannot be discharged and accumulates over time, turning the water black as ink. It has now become a storage place for all kinds of filth. Even though the weather is still cold, the stench is already unbearable. It is conceivable that in the hot summer, the foul air will be overwhelming, and epidemics are to be feared. Moreover, the foul mud and water are where mosquitoes and flies breed. This area is at the intersection of the Chinese and foreign concessions. At a time when new initiatives are being promoted, leaving this stain not only hinders the appearance of the city but also damages international credibility as foreigners spread the word about it. Therefore, we specifically request that your bureau approve sending specialists to the town to inspect the area and fill in the 30-odd zhang of river from the Tianyao Bridge to the Li Zongjing port, turning it into a level ground. This would keep the foul water from the east far away, and residents would be less likely to throw their waste into the river. The public's health and the elimination of epidemics would depend on this. Moreover, filling in the river surface would create a useful area. The funds would not be wasted, and the people would receive tangible benefits. We are eagerly awaiting your order."

The Tofu Industry in This City Will Raise Prices Starting May 1st 165

The Tofu Industry Guild of this city stated that due to the recent soaring prices of raw materials and increased costs, the old wholesale market prices were causing huge losses. At the same time, the draft industry regulations also needed to be discussed. Because the number of members present did not reach two-thirds of the total, the industry regulations could not be passed according to the law, so a discussion meeting was held instead. Tan Yueming, the chairman, reported that due to the soaring prices of soybeans recently, the costs had increased, and the old wholesale market prices were causing huge losses. As a result, no fewer than dozens of businesses in the same industry had ceased operations. At the same time, the guild's draft industry regulations had been prepared and urgently needed to be passed and submitted to the Social Affairs Bureau for record. For this reason, a general meeting of members was convened to discuss the matter together. Subsequently, the members present expressed their opinions separately and set new prices, which will be implemented uniformly by all businesses in the same industry starting on May 1st. The new price list is as follows: Tofu skin, 3 cents per sheet; old tofu, 100 wen per block; soft tofu, 1,200 wen per board, minimum 30 wen; coarse fried tofu, 24 cents per catty, minimum 60 wen; fine fried tofu, 32 cents per catty, minimum 60 wen; dried tofu skin, 22 cents per catty, 20 wen per sheet; fragrant (stinky) dried tofu, 30 cents per catty; fried tofu puff, 20 wen each; small square block, 10 wen each; fermented bean curd brick, 5 jiao per board; square cut, 3 jiao per board.

The Ministry of Industry and Commerce Explains the Accountants Ordinance; Handling Related Commissioned Matters in Different Locations Should Not Be Restricted by Article 16, Paragraph 1 of the Ordinance 166

The Shanghai Accountants Association stated that Article 8 of the Accountants Ordinance stipulates that "Before an accountant begins to practice, he shall submit an application form, together with his certificate, to the local industrial and commercial administrative authority for verification and registration in the Accountants Register," and Article 16, Paragraph 1 stipulates that "An accountant may not practice in a province or city without joining the Accountants Association of that province or city." According to these regulations, in addition to applying for registration with the local industrial and commercial administrative authority, an accountant must also join the Accountants Association of the province or city where he practices, otherwise he may not practice. This is clearly stipulated in the ordinance and is not open to doubt. However, sometimes an accountant in Location A is commissioned by a company in that location to be an auditor or liquidator, and the company has branches in Locations B, C, D, and E. After being commissioned, the accountant needs to go to the branches in Locations B, C, D, and E to handle matters related to the commission. It is doubtful whether he should join the Accountants Associations in each of these locations. The association submitted a request for clarification, and the Ministry of Industry and Commerce issued an instruction (Shang Zi No. 42998) explaining that "Since the accountant's business office is located in Location A, and the commissioned relationship with the company also occurred in Location A, then going to the branches in Locations B, C, D, and E to audit the accounts due to the related relationship is part of the work of handling the commissioned matter, and cannot be considered as practicing in each of these locations. However, establishing an office in a place other than the place of registration and membership in the association, soliciting commissioned matters, and handling them is different from the above situation and is still subject to the restrictions of Article 8 and Article 16 of the Accountants Ordinance," and so on.

This Year's Total Solar Eclipses in Japan and Russia; Our Country Will Send Personnel to Participate in Observations; Yu Qingsong and Others Will Go to Japan, Zhang Yuzhe and Others Will Go to Russia; Participating in International Solar Eclipse Observations for the First Time 168

Observing a total solar eclipse is of great importance to sciences such as astronomy, geography, and meteorology. When France was surrounded by Germany in the Tenth Century, French scientists flew in a balloon to break through the encirclement and observe the solar eclipse. The importance of this matter can be seen from this. On September 21st of the 30th year of the Republic of China, there will be a total solar eclipse passing through the Yellow River and Yangtze River basins of our country. At that time, various European countries will definitely come to China to observe it. Therefore, the Academia Sinica, Tsinghua University, the Astronomical Society, the Central Astronomical Observatory, and other organizations formed the Chinese Solar Eclipse Observation and Research Committee last year to prepare everything. This year, on June 19th, there will be a total solar eclipse in Japan and Russia. The committee has decided to send personnel to participate in the observations in order to practice and prepare for the observation of the total solar eclipse in the 30th year of the Republic of China. It is now learned that the Astronomical Observatory and the Chinese Astronomical Society have decided to send Yu Qingsong and Zheng Zungui to Hokkaido, Japan, and Zhang Yuzhe and Li Heng to Boli, Soviet Union, to participate in the observations. The observation items are divided into capturing solar corona images, solar radiation, meteorology, and geomagnetism. This is the first time that our country has sent representatives to participate in international solar eclipse observations. The four representatives are now preparing and will leave for Japan and Russia in the middle of next month. Because the mission is only to observe the solar eclipse, the time spent outside the country will not be very long.

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Telegraphs the Ministry of Finance, Requesting a Modified Method for Collecting the Full Tax on Broken Rice 172

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the Ministry of Finance of the Nanjing Executive Yuan's Customs Administration yesterday, stating, "On the 20th of this month, the Mixed Grain and Oilseed Cake Industry Guild sent a letter stating that the Jianghai Customs had issued a notice that starting on April 11th of this year, broken rice imports would be subject to the full tax, and those who had already declared imports and paid taxes on that day would not be exempted. We believe that the government has been collecting half tax on broken rice imports in order to benefit the common people. The lives of the common people are difficult to make ends meet. The quality of domestic rice is good, but the price is expensive, and their ability to buy grain is limited. Broken rice is light and cheap, so it provides a source of food. This year, the domestic rice production does not seem to be lacking, so there is no need to increase the tax. The reason why merchants continue to order broken rice is to meet the needs of the common people. When they ordered it, they all calculated based on the half tax, and after the order was placed, the goods were sold to various households at the half tax price. In short, the merchants' cost calculations are all based on the half tax. Now, the amount ordered, according to the registered number of the same industry, is 12,300 tons. After hearing the news, in addition to the approximately 7,000 to 8,000 tons that have already been sold to foreign producers at a loss, there are still 4,000 to 5,000 tons that are about to be imported, have already been shipped, or have not yet been shipped. If the full tax is paid on all of these, each bag will increase by about 1.9 yuan in domestic currency. The merchants' estimated losses are huge and unbearable given the current economic downturn. We believe that the merchants originally ordered broken rice to provide food for the common people, but the sudden increase in the import tax will lead to losses, which is unbearable from a humanitarian point of view. Moreover, the broken rice was ordered before the customs issued the notice, and according to the law, it should not be applied retroactively. Therefore, we specifically ask the association to quickly telegraph the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Finance, and the Customs Administration, and instruct the Jianghai Customs to continue to collect half tax on broken rice imported before April 11th of this year in order to alleviate the merchants' difficulties." Upon arrival, it was found that the import of broken rice is exclusively for the daily needs of the common people and has a wide sales range, so rice merchants import a large quantity of goods. Now, the change from half tax to full tax will increase the price per bag by nearly two yuan, making it difficult to sell and impossible to compensate. It is impossible to sell all of the imported or shipped goods abroad. If the full tax is suddenly levied according to the regulations, the rice merchants will face the risk of unbearable compensation, which may lead to difficulties in turnover and have a huge impact. Ningbo rice merchants have previously requested the Ningbo Chamber of Commerce to appeal. This time, the Shanghai mixed grain industry has followed suit with a request. The association, in light of the merchants' situation, believes that it is necessary to make a modification. It is appropriate to report the situation by telegram and request the Ministry (Department) (Administration) to review and approve the request of the guild. All imports of broken rice ordered before April 11th should be permitted to continue to be subject to half tax by the Jianghai Customs in order to give rice merchants a slight breather and ease the urgent situation. The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce respectfully submits.

Zhang Yier, a well-known comedian in the city, and his Zhang Yier Spirit Troupe, whose performances have been praised both locally and abroad, in order to enthusiastically support the purchase of an airplane as a birthday gift, will perform his masterpiece comedy opera "Happiness Comes to the Door" in its entirety at the Central Theater on the night of the 29th of this month. All ticket revenue, except for front-of-house expenses, will be donated. Yesterday, the association received a letter from the Zhenjiang branch of the China Tobacco Company, stating that colleagues have donated the funds saved from a banquet to purchase an airplane as a gift to the government in commemoration of Chairman Chiang's 50th birthday. The donations are as follows: Gu Youcheng, 4.27 yuan; Hua Hanchun, 1.22 yuan; Yuan Lianqing, 0.83 yuan; Wan Enyun, 0.83 yuan; Yang Jianyu, 0.74 yuan; Zhou Zikun, 1.86 yuan; Fang Guiqing, 0.56 yuan; Feng Jiafu, 0.83 yuan; Zhang Ganyong, 1.20 yuan; Yang Heting, 1.17 yuan; Chen Yuanqing and Xu Yunfeng, 0.74 yuan each; He Jingzhi, 0.63 yuan, totaling 15.62 yuan in national currency. The 44th joint meeting of the Shanghai Municipal Joint Association for Rent Reduction in All Districts decided to immediately notify the district associations to instruct their respective branches to begin raising funds to purchase an airplane for the celebration. Corpse's Wife Accuses Wang Shubao of Killing Ji Zhongtang Many Years Ago 180

Ji Zhongtang, a native of Funing, once served as a detective in the Municipal Public Security Bureau. In 1932, shortly after the end of the January 28th Incident in Shanghai, the order in Zhabei was chaotic. Ji Zhongtang was shot and killed. The local court sent personnel to investigate and record the case, pending the arrest of the murderer. Recently, the corpse's wife, Ji Wu, filed a complaint with the local court's prosecutor's office, accusing Wang Shubao, the owner of the Xiang Stage Theater in Zhabei and a native of Yancheng, of premeditatedly killing her husband, Ji Zhongtang, and requesting his arrest. After receiving the complaint, the court ordered the police to summon Wang Shubao and a related person, Zhang Xiaowanzi, for questioning the day before yesterday. After interrogation by Prosecutor Tang, they were ordered to be detained separately. Yesterday afternoon, lawyer Huang Zongqia (a native of Yancheng) was also summoned to court for questioning, and he was ordered to be released on bail pending a thorough investigation.

Case of Abuse of Maid Scheduled for Sentencing 181

Zhang Chen, a Ningbo woman, 30 years old, residing at No. 43, Bugao Lane, Yapei Road, French Concession, purchased a foster daughter named Caiqin, 7 years old, for 24 yuan through an intermediary on July 30th of last year. Unexpectedly, Chen was of a violent nature and often abused the girl. The day before yesterday, Chen beat Caiqin severely again. Neighbors heard the girl's cries of misery and questioned Chen, who not only refused to admit wrongdoing but also spoke rudely. The neighbors, feeling indignant on the girl's behalf, reported the incident to Patrolman No. 307, who brought Chen and Caiqin to the police station. Yesterday, they were sent to the First Criminal Court of the Second Special Court. The police lawyer first recounted the circumstances, stating that the hospital examination revealed that the girl was covered in injuries and burns and should be dealt with in accordance with Article 286, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Law. The judge ordered the bailiff to immediately send the girl to the forensic doctor for examination, which confirmed the presence of injuries. When questioned, Zhang Chen admitted that she had beaten Caiqin because Caiqin had stolen a cake from the table. She hired a lawyer to defend her. Judge Li concluded the debate and scheduled the sentencing for the 25th.

Robbers Attempt to Rob Bean Sprout Workshop 182

No. 66 Weining Road, Nanshi, is a three-story stone-gated building that looks like a mansion. It is currently rented by a Zhu from Pudong as a yellow bean sprout workshop. Yesterday (22nd) at 10:00 AM, Mr. Zhu's mother and daughter-in-law took the bean sprouts to the market to sell, leaving only two or three children at home to guard the door. The robbers, thinking that the house must be occupied by a wealthy family, stormed in with three or four people. One person used his hand to threaten the children and prevent them from making noise, while two or three people went upstairs to search, but found nothing. They left empty-handed. The third branch of the first district, upon hearing the news, immediately sent officers to investigate and reported the details to the bureau.

Weather Report 187

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:20 PM yesterday stated that the weather around Shandong is sunny with light northwest to southwest winds. The cloudy weather in the Yangtze River basin and here is gradually clearing up, with variable winds. The weather in the East China Sea and Taiwan is cloudy with rain and localized fog, and the wind direction is turning north. The center of the hurricane was within approximately 120 miles of 15 degrees north latitude and 122 degrees east longitude at 2:00 PM yesterday, moving northwest-north. The wind force is unknown. Also, within the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in the city was 66.6 degrees and the lowest was 61.9 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest temperature was 67.1 degrees and the lowest was 57.7 degrees.

Shanghai's Insurance Industry - Chief Editor of Chinese WeChat 188

(Shanghai Industrial and Commercial Overview No. 23)

French Companies: There are few French insurance companies in Shanghai, most of which are managed by Assurance France-Asiatizne. As for Compagnie France Americaine Dassmances, although it is registered with the French Consulate, in practice, American investment is greater, so it is not a purely French company. The details of the two companies are described separately below:

1. Assurance France-Asie Company: The company was founded in 1918 and is a limited company with a total capital of 7 million francs, and the paid-up capital is the same as the above amount. As of 1934, the reserve fund reached 22,623,872 francs, and the total assets reached 36,095,930 francs. It specializes in water, fire, automobile, and accident insurance. The head office is located in Paris, and the Shanghai branch is located at No. 1 Tianzhutang Street. The chairman is Mr. Fano R., and the general manager is Mr. Breen J. The annual operating income reaches more than 20 million francs. The profit in 1931 reached 61,001.36 francs, and the profit in 1932 reached 24,563.38 francs.

2. Franco-American Insurance Company: The company was founded in 1930, with its head office located at No. 7 Aiduya Road, Shanghai, the executive department at No. 17 The Bund, Shanghai, and its management offices in Annam are in Saigon, Hanoi, Haiphong, and Pnompenh. In China, there are offices in Tianjin, Qingdao, and Hankou. The paid-up capital is 3.5 million francs. As of the end of 1934, the statutory reserve fund was 107,131.87 francs, and the various claims reserve funds totaled 962,580.50 francs. Its total assets are about 5 million francs, but half of them are invested by American International Assurance Company. The company's business focuses on Annam ports and specializes in water, fire, automobile, and glass insurance. In 1934, it received a total of 2,468,159 francs in premiums. The chairman and supervisor is Siganl M.E., a Frenchman and director of Jianye Real Estate Company. Stan C.V. is the chairman of American International Assurance Company, and the general manager is Obakiewicg M.W. The deputy general manager is Mr. Zhu Jisheng.

D. Dutch Companies: Most Dutch insurance companies are represented by Shanghai Insurance Office and Java Sea & Fire Msurarice Co. Ltd. The details of the two companies are summarized below:

1. Shanghai Insurance Office: The head office is located at No. 299 Sichuan Road, Shanghai, and branches are located in Tianjin and Hankou. It manages water and fire insurance with a capital of 50,000 yuan. Its shareholders are Roelof anton Rrentan, a Dutchman, who once served as the Dutch Consul in Shanghai and is now the Far East General Manager of North America Insurance Company, and L.J. Klaili, another shareholder who is also the manager. The company's business is entirely of an agency nature. The annual premium income averages 200,000 yuan, and the annual net profit ranges from 23,000 to 56,000 yuan. Its agency companies include British America Assnr Co, Century Ins, Co. Ltel, Eagte Insurance Co Ltd, and 14 others.

2. Java Sea Insurance Company: The company was founded in 1861 and is a limited liability organization with a capital of 1.2 million francs. The head office is located in Batavia, and the Shanghai branch is located at No. 3 Xinkang Road. Its Shanghai manager is Mr. Van Somern H.C.A. The annual premium income is about 500,000 francs. In 1930, the profit was 3,968.43 francs. In 1931, the loss was 20,923.27 francs. In 1932, the profit was 60,847.15 francs.

E. Japanese and Other Companies: Japanese insurance companies in Shanghai are represented by Mitsui, Mitsubishi, and The Cornhill Ins. Ltd. The details of Mitsui and Mitsubishi are unknown. Although Kangtai is nominally established by the British, it is actually controlled by the Japanese. Its total capital is 500,000 pounds, and the paid-up capital is 250,000 pounds. The head office is located in London, and the Shanghai branch is located at No. 18 The Bund. The annual premium income is about 800,000 pounds. Its backstage supporter is Tokyo Insurance Co. Ltd. Shanghai Manager Aaki

As for companies of other nationalities such as Italian, Swiss, and Austrian, their influence in Shanghai is extremely weak, so I will not go into detail.

3. Overview of Chinese Insurance Companies

In recent years, due to the oppression of foreign forces, Chinese people have gradually tended to take out insurance with Chinese insurance companies. Furthermore, due to rural bankruptcy in recent years, funds have rapidly concentrated in cities. With the excess capital of the banking industry, in addition to competing for speculative businesses such as real estate and public bonds, they have also invested a large amount of idle capital in the insurance industry. As a result, Chinese insurance companies have been able to flourish. Some financiers, compradors of foreign insurance companies, and insurance clerks with insurance experience have all joined forces with those with financial resources to compete in establishing insurance companies. Therefore, there are as many as twenty Chinese insurance companies in recent times. A list of the various branch head offices in Shanghai is given below:

Sports News

Sino-British International Billiards: Chinese Team Wins Championship for Fourth Consecutive Year - Total Points: 2885 vs. 2717 189

Li Gongying Defeats Bernal 600 to 491 Yesterday - Bernal Creates New High Score Record of 79 Points

In the final match of the Fourth Sino-British International Billiards Championship, the billiards king Li Gongying made a final effort and defeated the Englishman Bernal with 600 points to 491 points. The Chinese team continued to retain the championship for the fourth consecutive year. The total score of the two teams was 2885 to 2717 points. The Chinese team won by a total of 168 points, the difference between the two sides not being too great, the game thus considered quite interesting. Yesterday, Bernal created a new high score record of 79 points on the 28th shot, and won the silver cup presented by Renji Foreign Firm. After the game, Mrs. Xu Junyi presented the award, and the Fourth Sino-British Billiards Championship came to a close amidst cheers. The billiards room of the Bank Club was packed with spectators yesterday, making it a grand occasion.

Different Fortunes: After the opening speech by Lin Kanghou, the game began. Bernal took the first shot, followed by Li Gongying. As a result of the first three shots, Bernal scored nothing, and had not recorded any points by the fifth. Li, on the other hand, scored a large number of 54 points on the third shot, leading by 73 points to 4 points. Bernal was still dejected. By the tenth shot, Li had scored another 58 points in one shot, accumulating a score of 172 to 32 points, a difference of 140 points, reflecting the extremely different fortunes of the two men.

New Record Created: Despite Bernal's determination to fight back under this huge deficit, he was unable to make progress. By the 28th shot, the score was 296 to 229. Bernal's opportunity was beginning to appear. With a very skillful shot, he scored a record 79 points in one go, catching up with a score of 296 to 269, with a difference of only 27 points. This was one of the most tense periods of the game.

Victory Confirmed: Although Bernal scored this large number of points, he was unable to continue in the same vein. Li Gongying then scored 46 and 36 points in two consecutive shots, once again taking the lead. On the 36th shot, Li scored 60 points, bringing the score to 458 to 363, widening the gap again. Bernal scored 65 points on the 41st shot, still lagging behind by 40 points. Then Li also tried to create a new high score, but his final shot only scored 64 points. At this point, the Chinese team's victory was confirmed. The Chinese team's remaining deficit was also small, and the hope of a new record for the billiards king could only be left for the future. The final score was 600 to 491, with a total of 49 shots.

Weightlifting and Martial Arts Preliminary for the World Games - Rescheduled for May 11th and 14th 193

The dates for the selection of weightlifting and martial arts athletes to participate in the World Games have been changed. The preliminary selection was previously scheduled for May 5th in Shanghai, the reselection for May 10th, and training was scheduled to begin on May 15th. Now, because the period between the preliminary selection and the training period is too long, resulting in excessive expenses for accommodation and food for personnel from various places staying in Shanghai, and to allow for sufficient preparation for the preliminary selection in various places, the selection dates have been rescheduled to May 11th for the preliminary selection and May 14th for the reselection. Training will still begin on May 15th. In this way, personnel staying in Shanghai will save time and money, and athletes from various places will have ample time to prepare.

Track and Field Training Class for Participation in the World Games Postponed - Liu Changchun, Zhou Changxing, and Six Others Have Already Registered - Class Will Begin After Shanghai Athletes Arrive in Beiping for Testing 195

(Beiping Special Dispatch) Registration for the track and field training class for China's participation in the World Games closed in Shanghai yesterday. However, the news about the track and field training class in recent days has been confusing and inconsistent. To obtain accurate information, the reporter went to Tsinghua University to inquire about everything. It turns out that those participating in the track and field training class had registered in Shanghai a few days ago, and registration only closed yesterday. According to a telegram from the National Sports Association to Mr. Ma Dehan, there were thirteen participants, but as of yesterday, only Peng Yongxin and Zhang Lingjia, who are at Tsinghua, and Liu Changchun and Zhou Changxing from Nanjing, Dong Shuzhao from Shanghai, and Zhang Yinming from Australia, Hebei, had registered in Beiping. Training was originally scheduled to begin yesterday, but Mr. Ma Dehan and Xia Xiang, the deputy instructor of the track and field training class, discussed that if training took place before the athletes' results were tested, the athletes would be too tired and the results would be affected. Therefore, it was decided to begin training after the results were tested. As for the date of the results test, if a large number of athletes who registered in Shanghai today (21st) can arrive in Beiping, then the test will be held on the 24th. If the athletes cannot arrive in Beiping today, the test will be postponed. The date for the start of training may be on the 27th of this month. The Tsinghua University Spring Sports Meeting is on the 25th, and the Tsinghua Commemoration Meeting is on the 26th, so it is difficult to start training then. The athletes who have already registered at Tsinghua, except for Zhang Lingjia, such as Liu Changchun, Dong Shuzhao, Zhou Changxing, Peng Yongxin, and Zhang Yinming, have been practicing on their own at the Tsinghua University field since yesterday.

The China Physical Education Federation's men's basketball league, this year's competition, began the day before yesterday at the Shenyuan basketball court. Yesterday was the second day, with a total of three matches. The first match was Fuzhong versus Fushi, a brotherly competition. Both sides were evenly matched, so the competition was exceptionally intense. In the first half, Fuzhong relied on coordinated teamwork to take the lead with a score of 12 to 9. The final result was 23 to 17, with Fuzhong winning. The second match was Guanghua versus Private Shang. The two teams were evenly matched, and the game was hard-fought. In the first half, Guanghua had a strong momentum, taking the lead with a score of 16 to 9. In the second half, Private Shang changed their strategy, and the entire team worked harder, winning with a score of 24 to 19. However, they still lost with an overall score of 35 to 33. The third match was Hujiang versus Minli. Hujiang's strength was formidable, and Minli was far from their match, so the game became one-sided. In the first half, Hujiang used deceptive tactics and had a blazing momentum, taking the lead with a huge score of 29 to 6. In the second half, Hujiang brought in a large number of fresh troops, and Minli took the opportunity to attack. However, due to their weaker overall strength, they still lost. The Eighth Annual Elementary School Games: Preliminary Rounds Being Organized in Each District. Lixing on the 30th, Gaoqiao on May 1st; Caojing and Yangsi Both Scheduled for May 2nd. 197

The eighth annual elementary school joint athletic meet of this city is scheduled to be held for three days from May 14th at the sports ground in the central district of the city. The Education Bureau has divided the city into 19 districts, and preliminary rounds will be held separately to select representatives to participate in the main meeting. Previous reports have given details of each situation. It is learned that the preparatory committees in each district have been appointed by the Education Bureau, and they are currently busily organizing the preliminary rounds. The preparatory situation in Lixing, Gaoqiao, Caojing, Yangsi and other districts is recorded as follows:

Lixing: The district held its first preparatory meeting yesterday at the Municipal Jiazi Elementary School. Attendees included Cao Huaqiu, Zhu Wenxin, Qu Siyan, Zhang Shuting, Zhu Mengqi, Jiang Mengxian, etc. Cao Huaqiu was the chairman, Jiang Mengxian the secretary. Resolutions: The preliminary selection date is set for April 30th, starting at 8:30 AM. If it rains, it will be postponed. The deadline for registration is April 27th at 5:00 PM. The cost of the preliminary rounds and participation in the main meeting will be shared by the schools in this district based on the number of grades. A fee of 2.5 yuan will be temporarily set for each grade. Each school must pay the fee when registering, otherwise the registration will be refused. In addition to the physical education teachers from the schools in this district, students from the Xinlu Normal School are also invited to help as referees. The referees are responsible for their own travel expenses and meals. The number of athlete representatives from this district is not yet specified, and will be decided after the preliminary rounds. The preparatory meeting will be convened again at 8:30 AM to determine the best athletes based on their performance. The sports supplies will be prepared by the preliminary meeting one day before the meeting. Each school will send someone directly to Xinlu Jiazi Elementary School to collect them, but safety pins must be brought by each athlete.

Gaoqiao: The district's preliminary selection meeting was convened by the chairman of the committee, Su Shude, on the 21st of this month. It was decided that the Gaoqiao district preliminary election meeting would be held on May 1st.

Caojing: Yesterday, the schools in the district gathered at the Huxi Qiuzhi Elementary School and immediately elected a General Affairs officer (Qiuzhi), an Accounting officer (Longhua), an Arrangement officer (Meilong), a Public Relations officer (Qiuzhi), and a Scheduling officer (Qiuzhi). The date for the preliminary rounds was set for May 2nd at 8:00 AM, to be held at Shangzhong in Wujia Lane. The deadline for athletes from each school to register is the 28th and registration should be submitted to Qiuzhi Elementary School. It is also heard that the next preparatory meeting is scheduled for 2:00 PM on the 24th at Qiuzhi.

Yangsi: The Yangsi district preliminary election meeting was held by Chairman Yang Huaichun, who recommended Wang Jiajie, Yuan Rong, Jiang Zuolin, and Li Yuanzhen to be preparatory members, and submitted their names to the Education Bureau for approval and appointment. The preparatory meeting was held yesterday at Yangsi Elementary School. It was decided to divide the work into four groups: administrative affairs, field events, track events, and venue. Preparations are being made and the preliminary election meeting is scheduled for May 2nd at the Yangsi Town Defense Corps drill ground. The meeting will prepare prizes in advance to encourage children's interest in sports.

Selection: Each school should follow the selection regulations stipulated by the Ministry of Education for selecting sports representatives. In case many schools are still unclear, the main points of the regulations are excerpted as follows. Students from each school who meet the following requirements may be selected as school sports representatives and should have their school provide a written certificate before participating in the sports meet: Those with good character; Those whose academic performance in all subjects in the previous semester is passing; Those who are physically strong and able to perform strenuous exercise; Those who have been formally enrolled in the school for more than one year.

Public Handball Match: China Victorious Yesterday 199

Zhu Kuan Overwhelms Anagavov; Sun Jialu Decisively Defeats Campbell

The third day of the China-West handball competition featured four singles matches. National team players Zhu Kuan and Sun Jialu participated. Handball king Zhu Kuan lived up to his reputation. In the first match against Anagavov, Mr. An was also a fierce competitor. In the first game, he fought tenaciously, but the result was still a victory for the handball king by a score of 21 to 15. In the second game, Zhu unleashed his might, and An's skills were exhausted. After a fierce battle, Zhu won 21 to 4, and An was almost completely defeated. The second game was F. Smith against Ti Quek Kay Ling. Mr. Ti did not give way, winning two games in a row with scores of 21 to 10 and 21 to 12. The third game was Sun Jialu against Campbell (temporarily switched with Smith against Bainat). The situation was lopsided. Sun relentlessly pressed forward, coming from all sides, leaving his opponent no chance to fight back. The scores were 21 to 10 and 21 to 1, a crisp and clean victory. The last game was C. Smith against Bainat. The two sides were evenly matched, and the competition was unusually tough. In the first game, neither side scored for more than ten rounds. Finally, Bainat won with a score of 21 to 15. Then, Smith won back the second game with a score of 21 to 19. In the last game, Smith's skill was ultimately slightly lacking, so Bainat won again with a score of 21 to 16. The competition continues today, with one singles game and two doubles games. Jiangsu Province Standardizes Scout Inspection and Camping Procedures: Jiangsu Provincial Council Issues an Order for All Counties to Comply 204

The Jiangsu Provincial Council of the Boy Scouts of China has stipulated a set of general rules for the organization of the Jiangsu Province county scout grand inspection and grand camping because the methods for the grand inspection and grand camping in each county are inconsistent. All county councils are ordered to comply. The original text is recorded as follows: A committee for the grand inspection and grand camping of boy scouts in each county shall be established with a number of members. In addition to the members of the county party department, or the commissioners, the county magistrate, the heads of various bureaus, and the directors of the boy scout council, who are ex officio directors, the remainder shall be appointed by the local council to serve as those who are enthusiastic about boy scout affairs. In counties where a council has not been established, they shall be appointed by the local party department. The powers of the committee for the grand inspection and grand camping of boy scouts in each county are as follows: A. Preparatory matters before the opening; B. Handling all matters during the grand inspection and grand camping; C. Concluding reporting matters after the closing. A standing committee of one to three members shall be established in the committee for the grand inspection and grand camping of boy scouts in each county, and shall be designated from among the members by the local council or the party department. The standing committee shall be divided into the following departments: A. General Affairs Department, B. Inspection Command Department, C. Campground Supervision Department, D. Curriculum Performance Department, E. Curriculum Competition Department. Each of the three departments of General Affairs, Curriculum Performance, and Curriculum Competition shall have one director, one deputy director, and a number of staff members, all of whom shall be appointed by the committee. The Inspection Command Department shall have one chief inspector, one deputy chief inspector, and three inspection commanders, all of whom shall be appointed by the committee. The Campground Supervision Department shall have one campground supervisor, one campground deputy supervisor, and a number of campground administrators, all of whom shall be appointed by the committee. The committee for the grand inspection and grand camping of boy scouts in each county shall have one chief referee, one chief inspection referee, one chief camping referee, one chief curriculum performance referee, one chief curriculum competition referee, and a number of referees. The chief referee shall be appointed by the Jiangsu Provincial Council, and the remainder shall be appointed by the local council or the party department. The committee for the grand inspection and grand camping of boy scouts in each county may, when necessary, establish a number of consultants, who shall be appointed by the local council or the party department as boy scout experts. Detailed rules shall be stipulated separately. These general rules may be amended at any time if there are any unfulfilled matters.

School Survey

Overview of Shanghai British School (5) 211

—Hu Zuyin

VI. Sports Facilities

The equipment of the school's gymnasium can be called the best in China. Even many domestic universities probably do not have such perfect facilities. The interior of the gymnasium is very large, and all kinds of indoor physical education activities or basketball games can be held in it. Next to the gymnasium, there are also sports instructor's offices, first aid stations, student bathrooms, changing rooms, toilets, etc. Each room is connected to water heating pipes, which can provide hot air; so even in the harsh winter, the school's students can change into thin sportswear and participate in various physical activities in the gymnasium without getting cold.

The equipment inside the gymnasium is really new and complete. Next to the wall on the right hand side of the entrance is a row of fixed indoor durable wall bars, with a long bench for the wall bars placed underneath. Another row is filled with many three-foot-long gymnastic bars. In front of it is installed a kind of large beam for silver chain body balance: it can be folded up when not in use, does not take up space, and can be moved out when needed. In another corner, there is a kind of iron frame with adjustable height. Behind it, there are two vertical ladders for practicing arm grip and climbing. On the left, there is another door leading to the playground. On both sides of the door, there are two machines for practicing arm and chest rowing movements. In another corner, there is a kind of leather bag and large ball for practicing boxing. Next to the door is a Milo weightlifting set, ranging from five pounds to three hundred pounds, with various weights available. Indoor running tracks are built on the upper floors around the gymnasium. Six long ropes and rings are hung on the outer pillars along the upper floor running track. Other various movable equipment, such as vaulting boxes, vaulting horses, parallel bars, sticks, mats, etc., are all available.

Because the school has a complete gymnasium, all kinds of physical activities can be taught and carried out. According to the school's sports instructor, the physical activities that the school's students usually participate in include: apparatus exercises, stunt exercises, ball games, track and field, boxing, Japanese judo, corrective gymnastics, and other temporary games and basic movement exercises. The students' physical progress is often recorded, and the students' parents are regularly reported to. (End)

As a result, each month fell by 0.003 or 0.004 yuan compared to the morning close. 3,500 bales of Shengyuan, 2,000 bales of Tonghe, 3,000 bales of Run Kang, 2,700 bales of Changfeng, 5,600 bales of Daji, 1,800 bales of Yuda, 2,500 bales of Shenji, and 2,700 bales of Renfeng, 2,700 bales of Taichang were sold. 3,700 bales of Dafu, 2,800 bales of Meiji, 3,100 bales of Juxing, 3,800 bales of Dafeng, 3,600 bales of Changhe, 2,100 bales of Tongfeng, 6,300 bales of Yuanyi, 2,800 bales of Yicheng, 2,000 bales of Dachangcheng, and 5,700 bales of Xincheng were bought. Seafood: Dongyang Shark Fin Sales Market is Quite Good 226

There are three types of black fin: the tail fin is called black hook, the fin on the back is called black skin, and the fin under the neck is called black sheep. The goods from the origin are usually sold as a whole set, that is, the hook, skin, and sheep are packaged together. The merchant sells them at a negotiated price. Occasionally, they are shipped in separate grades, but the number is small. The quality of those produced in the Hokkaido area of Japan is the best, because its roots are lighter and the fins are soft and glutinous and easy to swell in water, called Xiangguan goods. The goods from Kobe, Yokohama, Nagasaki, etc. have particularly heavy meat roots and reduced fin volume, so it is difficult to compare with Xiangguan, and the market price is also very different. There are also Taiwanese goods, the meat roots are light, but the slices are very small. Compared with Japanese goods, they are almost one to three. The sales of customer groups are also different. Therefore, no one has been heard to purchase whole goods. The original goods purchased by the experts must be selected and graded for sale. For example, black hooks are mostly sold in Tianjin, Hankou, Guangdong, and this street. Black skins are most popular in Nanjing and Suzhou. Black sheep are sold in various ports in Jiangbei. The current market price for top-grade Xiangguan black hooks is 210 yuan, 180-190 yuan for large pieces, and 150-160 yuan for medium pieces. Top-grade black skins are 160 yuan, large pieces are 130 yuan, and medium pieces are 100 yuan. Top-grade black sheep are 80 yuan, large pieces are 65 yuan, and medium pieces are 40 yuan. Goods from Yokohama, Kobe, and Nagasaki can be reduced by about 30 yuan for each grade. The price of Taiwanese top-grade black hooks is 120 yuan, top-grade black skins are 50 yuan, and top-grade black sheep are 20 yuan.
